The book I referred back to when deciding how I should act as king was The Prince.

Machiavelliâ€™s The Prince was called â€œthe devilâ€™s book,â€ and for hundreds of years after it was released, it was attacked by the Christian church. He also said, â€œWhen a prince is with his army, it is quite necessary for him to disregard the reputation of cruelty,â€ noting, â€œHannibal of Carthage faced no dissension among his troops or against himself, whether in victory or in defeat.
